37 class bitmap_image
38 {
39 public:
40 
41  enum channel_mode {
42  rgb_mode = 0,
43  bgr_mode = 1
44  };
45 
46  enum color_plane {
47  blue_plane = 0,
48  green_plane = 1,
49  red_plane = 2
50  };
51 
52  struct rgb_t
53  {
54  unsigned char red;
55  unsigned char green;
56  unsigned char blue;
57  };

59  bitmap_image()
60  : file_name_(""),
61  width_ (0),
62  height_ (0),
63  row_increment_ (0),
64  bytes_per_pixel_(3),
65  channel_mode_(bgr_mode)
66  {}

68  bitmap_image(const std::string& filename)
69  : file_name_(filename),
70  width_ (0),
71  height_ (0),
72  row_increment_ (0),
73  bytes_per_pixel_(0),
74  channel_mode_(bgr_mode)
75  {
76  load_bitmap();

102  bitmap_image& operator=(const bitmap_image& image)
103  {
104  if (this != &image)
105  {
106  file_name_ = image.file_name_;
107  bytes_per_pixel_ = image.bytes_per_pixel_;
108  width_ = image.width_;
109  height_ = image.height_;
110  row_increment_ = 0;
111  channel_mode_ = image.channel_mode_;
112  create_bitmap();
113  data_ = image.data_;
114  }
115 
116  return *this;
117  }
118 
119  inline bool operator!()
120  {
121  return (data_.size() == 0) ||
122  (width_ == 0) ||
123  (height_ == 0) ||
124  (row_increment_ == 0);
125  }

127  inline void clear(const unsigned char v = 0x00)
128  {
129  std::fill(data_.begin(), data_.end(), v);
130  }

132  inline unsigned char red_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y) const
133  {
134  return data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 2)];
135  }
136 
137  inline unsigned char green_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y) const
138  {
139  return data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 1)];
140  }
141 
142  inline unsigned char blue_channel (const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y) const
143  {
144  return data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 0)];
145  }

147  inline void red_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y, const unsigned char value)
148  {
149  data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 2)] = value;
150  }
151 
152  inline void green_channel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y, const unsigned char value)
153  {
154  data_[(y * row_increment_) + (x * bytes_per_pixel_ + 1)] = value;
155  }

157  inline void blue_channel (const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y, const unsigned char value)

162  inline unsigned char* row(unsigned int row_index) const
163  {
164  return const_cast<unsigned char*>(&data_[(row_index * row_increment_)]);
165  }

167  inline void get_pixel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y,
168  unsigned char& red,
169  unsigned char& green,
170  unsigned char& blue) const
171  {
172  const unsigned int y_offset = y * row_increment_;
173  const unsigned int x_offset = x * bytes_per_pixel_;
174  const unsigned int offset = y_offset + x_offset;
175 
176  blue = data_[offset + 0];
177  green = data_[offset + 1];
178  red = data_[offset + 2];
179  }
180 
181  template <typename RGB>
182  inline void get_pixel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y, RGB& colour) const
183  {
184  get_pixel(x, y, colour.red, colour.green, colour.blue);
185  }
186 
187  inline rgb_t get_pixel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y) const
188  {
189  rgb_t colour;
190  get_pixel(x, y, colour.red, colour.green, colour.blue);
191  return colour;
192  }

194  inline void set_pixel(const unsigned int x, const unsigned int y,
195  const unsigned char red,
196  const unsigned char green,
197  const unsigned char blue)
198  {
199  const unsigned int y_offset = y * row_increment_;
200  const unsigned int x_offset = x * bytes_per_pixel_;
201  const unsigned int offset = y_offset + x_offset;
202 
203  data_[offset + 0] = blue;
204  data_[offset + 1] = green;
205  data_[offset + 2] = red;
206  }

210  {
211  set_pixel(x, y, colour.red, colour.green, colour.blue);
212  }

214  inline bool copy_from(const bitmap_image& image)
215  {
216  if (
217  (image.height_ != height_) ||
218  (image.width_ != width_ )
219  )
220  {
221  return false;
222  }
223 
224  data_ = image.data_;
225 
226  return true;
227  }
228 
229  inline bool copy_from(const bitmap_image& source_image,
230  const unsigned int& x_offset,
231  const unsigned int& y_offset)
232  {
233  if ((x_offset + source_image.width_ ) > width_ ) { return false; }
234  if ((y_offset + source_image.height_) > height_) { return false; }
235 
236  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < source_image.height_; ++y)
237  {
238  unsigned char* itr1 = row(y + y_offset) + x_offset * bytes_per_pixel_;
239  const unsigned char* itr2 = source_image.row(y);
240  const unsigned char* itr2_end = itr2 + source_image.width_ * bytes_per_pixel_;
241 
242  std::copy(itr2, itr2_end, itr1);
243  }
244 
245  return true;
246  }
247 
248  inline bool region(const unsigned int& x ,
249  const unsigned int& y ,
250  const unsigned int& width ,
251  const unsigned int& height,
252  bitmap_image& dest_image ) const
253  {
254  if ((x + width ) > width_ ) { return false; }
255  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
256 
257  if (
258  (dest_image.width_ < width_ ) ||
259  (dest_image.height_ < height_)
260  )
261  {
262  dest_image.setwidth_height(width,height);
263  }
264 
265  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
266  {
267  unsigned char* itr1 = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
268  unsigned char* itr1_end = itr1 + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
269  unsigned char* itr2 = dest_image.row(r);
270 
271  std::copy(itr1, itr1_end, itr2);
272  }
273 
274  return true;
275  }
276 
277  inline bool roi_from_center(const unsigned int& cx ,
278  const unsigned int& cy ,
279  const unsigned int& width ,
280  const unsigned int& height,
281  bitmap_image& dest_image ) const
282  {
283  return region(cx - (width / 2), cy - (height / 2),
284  width, height,
285  dest_image);
286  }

288  inline bool set_region(const unsigned int& x ,
289  const unsigned int& y ,
290  const unsigned int& width ,
291  const unsigned int& height,
292  const unsigned char& value )
293  {
294  if ((x + width ) > width_ ) { return false; }
295  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
296 
297  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
298  {
299  unsigned char* itr = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
300  unsigned char* itr_end = itr + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
301 
302  std::fill(itr, itr_end, value);
303  }
304 
305  return true;
306  }
307 
308  inline bool set_region(const unsigned int& x ,
309  const unsigned int& y ,
310  const unsigned int& width ,
311  const unsigned int& height,
312  const color_plane color ,
313  const unsigned char& value )
314  {
315  if ((x + width ) > width_ ) { return false; }
316  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
317 
318  const unsigned int color_plane_offset = offset(color);
319 
320  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
321  {
322  unsigned char* itr = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_ + color_plane_offset;
323  unsigned char* itr_end = itr + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
324 
325  while (itr != itr_end)
326  {
327  *itr = value;
328  itr += bytes_per_pixel_;
329  }
330  }
331 
332  return true;
333  }
334 
335  inline bool set_region(const unsigned int& x ,
336  const unsigned int& y ,
337  const unsigned int& width ,
338  const unsigned int& height,
339  const unsigned char& red ,
340  const unsigned char& green ,
341  const unsigned char& blue )
342  {
343  if ((x + width ) > width_ ) { return false; }
344  if ((y + height) > height_) { return false; }
345 
346  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
347  {
348  unsigned char* itr = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
349  unsigned char* itr_end = itr + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
350 
351  while (itr != itr_end)
352  {
353  *(itr++) = blue;
354  *(itr++) = green;
355  *(itr++) = red;
356  }
357  }
358 
359  return true;
360  }
361 
362  void reflective_image(bitmap_image& image, const bool include_diagnols = false)
363  {
364  image.setwidth_height(3 * width_, 3 * height_, true);
365 
366  image.copy_from(*this, width_, height_);
367 
368  vertical_flip();
369 
370  image.copy_from(*this, width_, 0);
371  image.copy_from(*this, width_, 2 * height_);
372 
373  vertical_flip();
374  horizontal_flip();
375 
376  image.copy_from(*this, 0, height_);
377  image.copy_from(*this, 2 * width_, height_);
378 
379  horizontal_flip();
380 
381  if (include_diagnols)
382  {
383  bitmap_image tile = *this;
384 
385  tile.vertical_flip();
386  tile.horizontal_flip();
387 
388  image.copy_from(tile, 0, 0);
389  image.copy_from(tile, 2 * width_, 0);
390  image.copy_from(tile, 2 * width_, 2 * height_);
391  image.copy_from(tile, 0 , 2 * height_);
392  }
393  }

415  inline void setwidth_height(const unsigned int width,
416  const unsigned int height,
417  const bool clear = false)
418  {
419  data_.clear();
420  width_ = width;
421  height_ = height;
422 
423  create_bitmap();
424 
425  if (clear)
426  {
427  std::fill(data_.begin(), data_.end(), static_cast<unsigned char>(0x00));
428  }
429  }
430 
431  void save_image(const std::string& file_name) const
432  {
433  std::ofstream stream(file_name.c_str(),std::ios::binary);
434 
435  if (!stream)
436  {
437  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::save_image(): Error - Could not open file " << file_name << " for writing!" << std::endl;
438  return;
439  }
440 
441  bitmap_information_header bih;
442 
443  bih.width = width_;
444  bih.height = height_;
445  bih.bit_count = static_cast<unsigned short>(bytes_per_pixel_ << 3);
446  bih.clr_important = 0;
447  bih.clr_used = 0;
448  bih.compression = 0;
449  bih.planes = 1;
450  bih.size = bih.struct_size();
451  bih.x_pels_per_meter = 0;
452  bih.y_pels_per_meter = 0;
453  bih.size_image = (((bih.width * bytes_per_pixel_) + 3) & 0x0000FFFC) * bih.height;
454 
455  bitmap_file_header bfh;
456 
457  bfh.type = 19778;
458  bfh.size = bfh.struct_size() + bih.struct_size() + bih.size_image;
459  bfh.reserved1 = 0;
460  bfh.reserved2 = 0;
461  bfh.off_bits = bih.struct_size() + bfh.struct_size();
462 
463  write_bfh(stream,bfh);
464  write_bih(stream,bih);
465 
466  unsigned int padding = (4 - ((3 * width_) % 4)) % 4;
467  char padding_data[4] = { 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00 };
468 
469  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < height_; ++i)
470  {
471  const unsigned char* data_ptr = &data_[(row_increment_ * (height_ - i - 1))];
472 
473  stream.write(reinterpret_cast<const char*>(data_ptr), sizeof(unsigned char) * bytes_per_pixel_ * width_);
474  stream.write(padding_data,padding);
475  }
476 
477  stream.close();
478  }
479 
480  inline void set_all_ith_bits_low(const unsigned int bitr_index)
481  {
482  unsigned char mask = static_cast<unsigned char>(~(1 << bitr_index));
483 
484  for (unsigned char* itr = data(); itr != end(); ++itr)
485  {
486  *itr &= mask;
487  }
488  }
489 
490  inline void set_all_ith_bits_high(const unsigned int bitr_index)
491  {
492  unsigned char mask = static_cast<unsigned char>(1 << bitr_index);
493 
494  for (unsigned char* itr = data(); itr != end(); ++itr)
495  {
496  *itr |= mask;
497  }
498  }
499 
500  inline void set_all_ith_channels(const unsigned int& channel, const unsigned char& value)
501  {
502  for (unsigned char* itr = (data() + channel); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
503  {
504  *itr = value;
505  }
506  }

508  inline void set_channel(const color_plane color,const unsigned char& value)
509  {
510  for (unsigned char* itr = (data() + offset(color)); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
511  {
512  *itr = value;
513  }
514  }
515 
516  inline void ror_channel(const color_plane color, const unsigned int& ror)
517  {
518  for (unsigned char* itr = (data() + offset(color)); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
519  {
520  *itr = static_cast<unsigned char>(((*itr) >> ror) | ((*itr) << (8 - ror)));
521  }
522  }
523 
524  inline void set_all_channels(const unsigned char& value)
525  {
526  for (unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); )
527  {
528  *(itr++) = value;
529  }
530  }

532  inline void set_all_channels(const unsigned char& r_value,
533  const unsigned char& g_value,
534  const unsigned char& b_value)
535  {
536  for (unsigned char* itr = (data() + 0); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
537  {
538  *(itr + 0) = b_value;
539  *(itr + 1) = g_value;
540  *(itr + 2) = r_value;
541  }
542  }

544  inline void invert_color_planes()
545  {
546  for (unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); *itr = ~(*itr), ++itr);
547  }
548 
549  inline void add_to_color_plane(const color_plane color, const unsigned char& value)
550  {
551  for (unsigned char* itr = (data() + offset(color)); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
552  {
553  (*itr) += value;
554  }
555  }

557  inline void convert_to_grayscale()
558  {
559  double r_scaler = 0.299;
560  double g_scaler = 0.587;
561  double b_scaler = 0.114;
562 
563  if (rgb_mode == channel_mode_)
564  {
565  std::swap(r_scaler, b_scaler);
566  }
567 
568  for (unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); )
569  {
570  unsigned char gray_value = static_cast<unsigned char>
571  (
572  (r_scaler * (*(itr + 2))) +
573  (g_scaler * (*(itr + 1))) +
574  (b_scaler * (*(itr + 0)))
575  );
576 
577  *(itr++) = gray_value;
578  *(itr++) = gray_value;
579  *(itr++) = gray_value;
580  }
581  }
582 
583  inline const unsigned char* data() const
584  {
585  return data_.data();
586  }
587 
588  inline unsigned char* data()
589  {
590  return const_cast<unsigned char*>(data_.data());
591  }
592 
593  inline void bgr_to_rgb()
594  {
595  if ((bgr_mode == channel_mode_) && (3 == bytes_per_pixel_))
596  {
597  reverse_channels();
598  channel_mode_ = rgb_mode;
599  }
600  }
601 
602  inline void rgb_to_bgr()
603  {
604  if ((rgb_mode == channel_mode_) && (3 == bytes_per_pixel_))
605  {
606  reverse_channels();
607  channel_mode_ = bgr_mode;
608  }
609  }
610 
611  inline void reverse()
612  {
613  unsigned char* itr1 = data();
614  unsigned char* itr2 = end() - bytes_per_pixel_;
615 
616  while (itr1 < itr2)
617  {
618  for (std::size_t i = 0; i < bytes_per_pixel_; ++i)
619  {
620  unsigned char* citr1 = itr1 + i;
621  unsigned char* citr2 = itr2 + i;
622 
623  std::swap(*citr1,*citr2);
624  }
625 
626  itr1 += bytes_per_pixel_;
627  itr2 -= bytes_per_pixel_;
628  }
629  }
630 
631  inline void horizontal_flip()
632  {
633  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < height_; ++y)
634  {
635  unsigned char* itr1 = row(y);
636  unsigned char* itr2 = itr1 + row_increment_ - bytes_per_pixel_;
637 
638  while (itr1 < itr2)
639  {
640  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < bytes_per_pixel_; ++i)
641  {
642  unsigned char* p1 = (itr1 + i);
643  unsigned char* p2 = (itr2 + i);
644 
645  std::swap(*p1,*p2);
646  }
647 
648  itr1 += bytes_per_pixel_;
649  itr2 -= bytes_per_pixel_;
650  }
651  }
652  }
653 
654  inline void vertical_flip()
655  {
656  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < (height_ / 2); ++y)
657  {
658  unsigned char* itr1 = row(y);
659  unsigned char* itr2 = row(height_ - y - 1);
660 
661  for (std::size_t x = 0; x < row_increment_; ++x)
662  {
663  std::swap(*(itr1 + x),*(itr2 + x));
664  }
665  }
666  }
667 
668  inline void export_color_plane(const color_plane color, unsigned char* image)
669  {
670  for (unsigned char* itr = (data() + offset(color)); itr < end(); ++image, itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
671  {
672  (*image) = (*itr);
673  }
674  }
675 
676  inline void export_color_plane(const color_plane color, bitmap_image& image)
677  {
678  if (
679  (width_ != image.width_ ) ||
680  (height_ != image.height_)
681  )
682  {
683  image.setwidth_height(width_,height_);
684  }
685 
686  image.clear();
687 
688  unsigned char* itr1 = (data() + offset(color));
689  unsigned char* itr1_end = end();
690  unsigned char* itr2 = (image.data() + offset(color));
691 
692  while (itr1 < itr1_end)
693  {
694  (*itr2) = (*itr1);
695 
696  itr1 += bytes_per_pixel_;
697  itr2 += bytes_per_pixel_;
698  }
699  }
700 
701  inline void export_response_image(const color_plane color, double* response_image)
702  {
703  double* resp_itr = response_image;
704 
705  for (unsigned char* itr = (data() + offset(color)); itr < end(); ++response_image, itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
706  {
707  *(resp_itr++) = (1.0 * (*itr)) / 256.0;
708  }
709  }
710 
711  inline void export_gray_scale_response_image(double* response_image) const
712  {
713  double* resp_itr = response_image;
714 
715  for (const unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
716  {
717  unsigned char gray_value = static_cast<unsigned char>
718  (
719  (0.299 * (*(itr + 2))) +
720  (0.587 * (*(itr + 1))) +
721  (0.114 * (*(itr + 0)))
722  );
723 
724  *(resp_itr++) = (1.0 * gray_value) / 256.0;
725  }
726  }
727 
728  inline void export_rgb(double* red, double* green, double* blue) const
729  {
730  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
731  return;
732 
733  for (const unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
734  {
735  (*blue ) = (1.0 * (*(itr++))) / 256.0;
736  (*green) = (1.0 * (*(itr++))) / 256.0;
737  (*red ) = (1.0 * (*(itr++))) / 256.0;
738  }
739  }
740 
741  inline void export_rgb(float* red, float* green, float* blue) const
742  {
743  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
744  return;
745 
746  for (const unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
747  {
748  (*blue ) = (1.0f * (*(itr++))) / 256.0f;
749  (*green) = (1.0f * (*(itr++))) / 256.0f;
750  (*red ) = (1.0f * (*(itr++))) / 256.0f;
751  }
752  }
753 
754  inline void export_rgb(unsigned char* red, unsigned char* green, unsigned char* blue) const
755  {
756  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
757  return;
758 
759  for (const unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); ++red, ++green, ++blue)
760  {
761  (*blue ) = *(itr++);
762  (*green) = *(itr++);
763  (*red ) = *(itr++);
764  }
765  }
766 
767  inline void export_ycbcr(double* y, double* cb, double* cr) const
768  {
769  if (bgr_mode != channel_mode_)
770  return;
771 
772  for (const unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); ++y, ++cb, ++cr)
773  {
774  const double blue = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
775  const double green = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
776  const double red = (1.0 * (*(itr++)));
777 
778  ( *y) = clamp<double>( 16.0 + (1.0/256.0) * ( 65.738 * red + 129.057 * green + 25.064 * blue),1.0,254);
779  (*cb) = clamp<double>(128.0 + (1.0/256.0) * (- 37.945 * red - 74.494 * green + 112.439 * blue),1.0,254);
780  (*cr) = clamp<double>(128.0 + (1.0/256.0) * ( 112.439 * red - 94.154 * green - 18.285 * blue),1.0,254);
781  }
782  }

935  inline void subsample(bitmap_image& dest) const
936  {
937  /*
938  Half sub-sample of original image.
939  */
940  unsigned int w = 0;
941  unsigned int h = 0;
942 
943  bool odd_width = false;
944  bool odd_height = false;
945 
946  if (0 == (width_ % 2))
947  w = width_ / 2;
948  else
949  {
950  w = 1 + (width_ / 2);
951  odd_width = true;
952  }
953 
954  if (0 == (height_ % 2))
955  h = height_ / 2;
956  else
957  {
958  h = 1 + (height_ / 2);
959  odd_height = true;
960  }
961 
962  unsigned int horizontal_upper = (odd_width) ? (w - 1) : w;
963  unsigned int vertical_upper = (odd_height) ? (h - 1) : h;
964 
965  dest.setwidth_height(w,h);
966  dest.clear();
967 
968  unsigned char* s_itr[3];
969  const unsigned char* itr1[3];
970  const unsigned char* itr2[3];
971 
972  s_itr[0] = dest.data() + 0;
973  s_itr[1] = dest.data() + 1;
974  s_itr[2] = dest.data() + 2;
975 
976  itr1[0] = data() + 0;
977  itr1[1] = data() + 1;
978  itr1[2] = data() + 2;
979 
980  itr2[0] = data() + row_increment_ + 0;
981  itr2[1] = data() + row_increment_ + 1;
982  itr2[2] = data() + row_increment_ + 2;
983 
984  unsigned int total = 0;
985 
986  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < vertical_upper; ++j)
987  {
988  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i)
989  {
990  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
991  {
992  total = 0;
993  total += *(itr1[k]);
994  total += *(itr1[k]);
995  total += *(itr2[k]);
996  total += *(itr2[k]);
997 
998  itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
999  itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1000  itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1001  itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1002 
1003  *(s_itr[k]) = static_cast<unsigned char>(total >> 2);
1004  }
1005  }
1006 
1007  if (odd_width)
1008  {
1009  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
1010  {
1011  total = 0;
1012  total += *(itr1[k]);
1013  total += *(itr2[k]);
1014 
1015  itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1016  itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1017 
1018  *(s_itr[k]) = static_cast<unsigned char>(total >> 1);
1019  }
1020  }
1021 
1022  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; ++k)
1023  {
1024  itr1[k] += row_increment_;
1025  }
1026 
1027  if (j != (vertical_upper - 1))
1028  {
1029  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; ++k)
1030  {
1031  itr2[k] += row_increment_;
1032  }
1033  }
1034  }
1035 
1036  if (odd_height)
1037  {
1038  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i)
1039  {
1040  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
1041  {
1042  total = 0;
1043  total += *(itr1[k]);
1044  total += *(itr2[k]);
1045 
1046  itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1047  itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1048 
1049  *(s_itr[k]) = static_cast<unsigned char>(total >> 1);
1050  }
1051  }
1052 
1053  if (odd_width)
1054  {
1055  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; ++k)
1056  {
1057  (*(s_itr[k])) = *(itr1[k]);
1058  }
1059  }
1060  }
1061  }
1062 
1063  inline void upsample(bitmap_image& dest) const
1064  {
1065  /*
1066  2x up-sample of original image.
1067  */
1068 
1069  dest.setwidth_height(2 * width_ ,2 * height_);
1070  dest.clear();
1071 
1072  const unsigned char* s_itr[3];
1073  unsigned char* itr1[3];
1074  unsigned char* itr2[3];
1075 
1076  s_itr[0] = data() + 0;
1077  s_itr[1] = data() + 1;
1078  s_itr[2] = data() + 2;
1079 
1080  itr1[0] = dest.data() + 0;
1081  itr1[1] = dest.data() + 1;
1082  itr1[2] = dest.data() + 2;
1083 
1084  itr2[0] = dest.data() + dest.row_increment_ + 0;
1085  itr2[1] = dest.data() + dest.row_increment_ + 1;
1086  itr2[2] = dest.data() + dest.row_increment_ + 2;
1087 
1088  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < height_; ++j)
1089  {
1090  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < width_; ++i)
1091  {
1092  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; s_itr[k] += bytes_per_pixel_, ++k)
1093  {
1094  *(itr1[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1095  *(itr1[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr1[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1096 
1097  *(itr2[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1098  *(itr2[k]) = *(s_itr[k]); itr2[k] += bytes_per_pixel_;
1099  }
1100  }
1101 
1102  for (unsigned int k = 0; k < bytes_per_pixel_; ++k)
1103  {
1104  itr1[k] += dest.row_increment_;
1105  itr2[k] += dest.row_increment_;
1106  }
1107  }
1108  }
1109 
1110  inline void alpha_blend(const double& alpha, const bitmap_image& image)
1111  {
1112  if (
1113  (image.width_ != width_ ) ||
1114  (image.height_ != height_)
1115  )
1116  {
1117  return;
1118  }
1119 
1120  if ((alpha < 0.0) || (alpha > 1.0))
1121  {
1122  return;
1123  }
1124 
1125  unsigned char* itr1 = data();
1126  const unsigned char* itr1_end = end();
1127  const unsigned char* itr2 = image.data();
1128 
1129  double alpha_compliment = 1.0 - alpha;
1130 
1131  while (itr1 != itr1_end)
1132  {
1133  *(itr1) = static_cast<unsigned char>((alpha * (*itr2)) + (alpha_compliment * (*itr1)));
1134  ++itr1;
1135  ++itr2;
1136  }
1137  }
1138 
1139  inline double psnr(const bitmap_image& image)
1140  {
1141  if (
1142  (image.width_ != width_ ) ||
1143  (image.height_ != height_)
1144  )
1145  {
1146  return 0.0;
1147  }
1148 
1149  const unsigned char* itr1 = data();
1150  const unsigned char* itr2 = image.data();
1151 
1152  double mse = 0.0;
1153 
1154  while (itr1 != end())
1155  {
1156  const double v = (static_cast<double>(*itr1) - static_cast<double>(*itr2));
1157 
1158  mse += v * v;
1159  ++itr1;
1160  ++itr2;
1161  }
1162 
1163  if (mse <= 0.0000001)
1164  {
1165  return 1000000.0;
1166  }
1167  else
1168  {
1169  mse /= (3.0 * width_ * height_);
1170 
1171  return 20.0 * std::log10(255.0 / std::sqrt(mse));
1172  }
1173  }
1174 
1175  inline double psnr(const unsigned int& x,
1176  const unsigned int& y,
1177  const bitmap_image& image)
1178  {
1179  if ((x + image.width() ) > width_ ) { return 0.0; }
1180  if ((y + image.height()) > height_) { return 0.0; }
1181 
1182  double mse = 0.0;
1183 
1184  const unsigned int height = image.height();
1185  const unsigned int width = image.width();
1186 
1187  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
1188  {
1189  const unsigned char* itr1 = row(r + y) + x * bytes_per_pixel_;
1190  const unsigned char* itr1_end = itr1 + (width * bytes_per_pixel_);
1191  const unsigned char* itr2 = image.row(r);
1192 
1193  while (itr1 != itr1_end)
1194  {
1195  double v = (static_cast<double>(*itr1) - static_cast<double>(*itr2));
1196  mse += v * v;
1197  ++itr1;
1198  ++itr2;
1199  }
1200  }
1201 
1202  if (mse <= 0.0000001)
1203  {
1204  return 1000000.0;
1205  }
1206  else
1207  {
1208  mse /= (3.0 * image.width() * image.height());
1209  return 20.0 * std::log10(255.0 / std::sqrt(mse));
1210  }
1211  }
1212 
1213  inline void histogram(const color_plane color, double hist[256]) const
1214  {
1215  std::fill(hist, hist + 256, 0.0);
1216 
1217  for (const unsigned char* itr = (data() + offset(color)); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
1218  {
1219  ++hist[(*itr)];
1220  }
1221  }
1222 
1223  inline void histogram_normalized(const color_plane color, double hist[256]) const
1224  {
1225  histogram(color,hist);
1226 
1227  double* h_itr = hist;
1228  const double* h_end = hist + 256;
1229  const double pixel_count = static_cast<double>(width_ * height_);
1230 
1231  while (h_end != h_itr)
1232  {
1233  *(h_itr++) /= pixel_count;
1234  }
1235  }
1236 
1237  inline unsigned int offset(const color_plane color) const
1238  {
1239  switch (channel_mode_)
1240  {
1241  case rgb_mode : {
1242  switch (color)
1243  {
1244  case red_plane : return 0;
1245  case green_plane : return 1;
1246  case blue_plane : return 2;
1247  default : return std::numeric_limits<unsigned int>::max();
1248  }
1249  }
1250 
1251  case bgr_mode : {
1252  switch (color)
1253  {
1254  case red_plane : return 2;
1255  case green_plane : return 1;
1256  case blue_plane : return 0;
1257  default : return std::numeric_limits<unsigned int>::max();
1258  }
1259  }
1260 
1261  default : return std::numeric_limits<unsigned int>::max();
1262  }
1263  }
1264 
1265  inline void incremental()
1266  {
1267  unsigned char current_color = 0;
1268 
1269  for (unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end();)
1270  {
1271  (*itr++) = (current_color);
1272  (*itr++) = (current_color);
1273  (*itr++) = (current_color);
1274 
1275  ++current_color;
1276  }
1277  }
1278 
1279  inline void reverse_channels()
1280  {
1281  if (3 != bytes_per_pixel_)
1282  return;
1283 
1284  for (unsigned char* itr = data(); itr < end(); itr += bytes_per_pixel_)
1285  {
1286  std::swap(*(itr + 0),*(itr + 2));
1287  }
1288  }
1289 
1290 private:
1291 
1292  inline const unsigned char* end() const
1293  {
1294  return data_.data() + data_.size();
1295  }
1296 
1297  inline unsigned char* end()
1298  {
1299  return const_cast<unsigned char*>(data() + data_.size());
1300  }

1302  struct bitmap_file_header
1303  {
1304  unsigned short type;
1305  unsigned int size;
1306  unsigned short reserved1;
1307  unsigned short reserved2;
1308  unsigned int off_bits;
1309 
1310  unsigned int struct_size() const
1311  {
1312  return sizeof(type ) +
1313  sizeof(size ) +
1314  sizeof(reserved1) +
1315  sizeof(reserved2) +
1316  sizeof(off_bits ) ;
1317  }
1318 
1319  void clear()
1320  {
1321  std::memset(this, 0x00, sizeof(bitmap_file_header));
1322  }
1323  };
1324 
1325  struct bitmap_information_header
1326  {

1328  unsigned int width;
1329  unsigned int height;
1330  unsigned short planes;
1331  unsigned short bit_count;
1332  unsigned int compression;
1333  unsigned int size_image;
1334  unsigned int x_pels_per_meter;
1335  unsigned int y_pels_per_meter;
1336  unsigned int clr_used;
1337  unsigned int clr_important;
1338 
1339  unsigned int struct_size() const
1340  {
1341  return sizeof(size ) +
1342  sizeof(width ) +
1343  sizeof(height ) +
1344  sizeof(planes ) +
1345  sizeof(bit_count ) +
1346  sizeof(compression ) +
1347  sizeof(size_image ) +
1348  sizeof(x_pels_per_meter) +
1349  sizeof(y_pels_per_meter) +
1350  sizeof(clr_used ) +
1351  sizeof(clr_important ) ;
1352  }
1353 
1354  void clear()
1355  {
1356  std::memset(this, 0x00, sizeof(bitmap_information_header));
1357  }
1358  };
1359 
1360  inline bool big_endian() const
1361  {
1362  unsigned int v = 0x01;
1363 
1364  return (1 != reinterpret_cast<char*>(&v)[0]);
1365  }
1366 
1367  inline unsigned short flip(const unsigned short& v) const
1368  {
1369  return ((v >> 8) | (v << 8));
1370  }
1371 
1372  inline unsigned int flip(const unsigned int& v) const
1373  {
1374  return (
1375  ((v & 0xFF000000) >> 0x18) |
1376  ((v & 0x000000FF) << 0x18) |
1377  ((v & 0x00FF0000) >> 0x08) |
1378  ((v & 0x0000FF00) << 0x08)
1379  );
1380  }
1381 
1382  template <typename T>
1383  inline void read_from_stream(std::ifstream& stream,T& t)
1384  {
1385  stream.read(reinterpret_cast<char*>(&t),sizeof(T));
1386  }
1387 
1388  template <typename T>
1389  inline void write_to_stream(std::ofstream& stream,const T& t) const
1390  {
1391  stream.write(reinterpret_cast<const char*>(&t),sizeof(T));
1392  }
1393 
1394  inline void read_bfh(std::ifstream& stream, bitmap_file_header& bfh)
1395  {
1396  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.type );
1397  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.size );
1398  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.reserved1);
1399  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.reserved2);
1400  read_from_stream(stream,bfh.off_bits );
1401 
1402  if (big_endian())
1403  {
1404  bfh.type = flip(bfh.type );
1405  bfh.size = flip(bfh.size );
1406  bfh.reserved1 = flip(bfh.reserved1);
1407  bfh.reserved2 = flip(bfh.reserved2);
1408  bfh.off_bits = flip(bfh.off_bits );
1409  }
1410  }
1411 
1412  inline void write_bfh(std::ofstream& stream, const bitmap_file_header& bfh) const
1413  {
1414  if (big_endian())
1415  {
1416  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.type ));
1417  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.size ));
1418  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.reserved1));
1419  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.reserved2));
1420  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bfh.off_bits ));
1421  }
1422  else
1423  {
1424  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.type );
1425  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.size );
1426  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.reserved1);
1427  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.reserved2);
1428  write_to_stream(stream,bfh.off_bits );
1429  }
1430  }
1431 
1432  inline void read_bih(std::ifstream& stream,bitmap_information_header& bih)
1433  {
1434  read_from_stream(stream,bih.size );
1435  read_from_stream(stream,bih.width );
1436  read_from_stream(stream,bih.height );
1437  read_from_stream(stream,bih.planes );
1438  read_from_stream(stream,bih.bit_count );
1439  read_from_stream(stream,bih.compression );
1440  read_from_stream(stream,bih.size_image );
1441  read_from_stream(stream,bih.x_pels_per_meter);
1442  read_from_stream(stream,bih.y_pels_per_meter);
1443  read_from_stream(stream,bih.clr_used );
1444  read_from_stream(stream,bih.clr_important );
1445 
1446  if (big_endian())
1447  {
1448  bih.size = flip(bih.size );
1449  bih.width = flip(bih.width );
1450  bih.height = flip(bih.height );
1451  bih.planes = flip(bih.planes );
1452  bih.bit_count = flip(bih.bit_count );
1453  bih.compression = flip(bih.compression );
1454  bih.size_image = flip(bih.size_image );
1455  bih.x_pels_per_meter = flip(bih.x_pels_per_meter);
1456  bih.y_pels_per_meter = flip(bih.y_pels_per_meter);
1457  bih.clr_used = flip(bih.clr_used );
1458  bih.clr_important = flip(bih.clr_important );
1459  }
1460  }
1461 
1462  inline void write_bih(std::ofstream& stream, const bitmap_information_header& bih) const
1463  {
1464  if (big_endian())
1465  {
1466  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.size ));
1467  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.width ));
1468  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.height ));
1469  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.planes ));
1470  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.bit_count ));
1471  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.compression ));
1472  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.size_image ));
1473  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.x_pels_per_meter));
1474  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.y_pels_per_meter));
1475  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.clr_used ));
1476  write_to_stream(stream,flip(bih.clr_important ));

1478  else

1480  write_to_stream(stream,bih.size );
1481  write_to_stream(stream,bih.width );
1482  write_to_stream(stream,bih.height );
1483  write_to_stream(stream,bih.planes );
1484  write_to_stream(stream,bih.bit_count );
1485  write_to_stream(stream,bih.compression );
1486  write_to_stream(stream,bih.size_image );
1487  write_to_stream(stream,bih.x_pels_per_meter);
1488  write_to_stream(stream,bih.y_pels_per_meter);
1489  write_to_stream(stream,bih.clr_used );
1490  write_to_stream(stream,bih.clr_important );
1491  }

1494  inline std::size_t file_size(const std::string& file_name) const
1495  {
1496  std::ifstream file(file_name.c_str(),std::ios::in | std::ios::binary);
1497  if (!file) return 0;
1498  file.seekg (0, std::ios::end);
1499  return static_cast<std::size_t>(file.tellg());
1500  }
1501 
1502  void create_bitmap()
1503  {
1504  row_increment_ = width_ * bytes_per_pixel_;
1505  data_.resize(height_ * row_increment_);
1506  }
1507 
1508  void load_bitmap()
1509  {
1510  std::ifstream stream(file_name_.c_str(),std::ios::binary);
1511 
1512  if (!stream)
1513  {
1514  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - file " << file_name_ << " not found!" << std::endl;
1515  return;
1516  }
1517 
1518  width_ = 0;
1519  height_ = 0;
1520 
1521  bitmap_file_header bfh;
1522  bitmap_information_header bih;
1523 
1524  bfh.clear();
1525  bih.clear();
1526 
1527  read_bfh(stream,bfh);
1528  read_bih(stream,bih);
1529 
1530  if (bfh.type != 19778)
1531  {
1532  bfh.clear();
1533  bih.clear();
1534 
1535  stream.close();
1536 
1537  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - Invalid type value " << bfh.type << " expected 19778." << std::endl;
1538  return;
1539  }
1540 
1541  if (bih.bit_count != 24)
1542  {
1543  bfh.clear();
1544  bih.clear();
1545 
1546  stream.close();
1547 
1548  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - Invalid bit depth " << bih.bit_count << " expected 24." << std::endl;
1549 
1550  return;
1551  }
1552 
1553  if (bih.size != bih.struct_size())
1554  {
1555  bfh.clear();
1556  bih.clear();
1557 
1558  stream.close();
1559 
1560  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - Invalid BIH size " << bih.size << " expected " << bih.struct_size() << std::endl;
1561 
1562  return;
1563  }
1564 
1565  width_ = bih.width;
1566  height_ = bih.height;
1567 
1568  bytes_per_pixel_ = bih.bit_count >> 3;
1569 
1570  unsigned int padding = (4 - ((3 * width_) % 4)) % 4;
1571  char padding_data[4] = {0,0,0,0};
1572 
1573  std::size_t bitmap_file_size = file_size(file_name_);
1574 
1575  std::size_t bitmap_logical_size = (height_ * width_ * bytes_per_pixel_) +
1576  (height_ * padding) +
1577  bih.struct_size() +
1578  bfh.struct_size() ;
1579 
1580  if (bitmap_file_size != bitmap_logical_size)
1581  {
1582  bfh.clear();
1583  bih.clear();
1584 
1585  stream.close();
1586 
1587  std::cerr << "bitmap_image::load_bitmap() ERROR: bitmap_image - Mismatch between logical and physical sizes of bitmap. " <<
1588  "Logical: " << bitmap_logical_size << " " <<
1589  "Physical: " << bitmap_file_size << std::endl;
1590 
1591  return;
1592  }
1593 
1594  create_bitmap();
1595 
1596  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < height_; ++i)
1597  {
1598  unsigned char* data_ptr = row(height_ - i - 1); // read in inverted row order
1599 
1600  stream.read(reinterpret_cast<char*>(data_ptr), sizeof(char) * bytes_per_pixel_ * width_);
1601  stream.read(padding_data,padding);
1602  }
1603  }
1604 
1605  template <typename T>
1606  inline T clamp(const T& v, const T& lower_range, const T& upper_range) const
1607  {
1608  if (v < lower_range)
1609  return lower_range;
1610  else if (v > upper_range)
1611  return upper_range;
1612  else
1613  return v;
1614  }
1615 
1616  std::string file_name_;
1617  unsigned int width_;
1618  unsigned int height_;
1619  unsigned int row_increment_;
1620  unsigned int bytes_per_pixel_;
1621  channel_mode channel_mode_;
1622  std::vector<unsigned char> data_;
1623 };

1627 inline bool operator==(const rgb_t& c0, const rgb_t& c1)
1628 {
1629  return (c0.red == c1 .red) &&
1630  (c0.green == c1.green) &&
1631  (c0.blue == c1 .blue) ;
1632 }
1633 
1634 inline bool operator!=(const rgb_t& c0, const rgb_t& c1)
1635 {
1636  return (c0.red != c1 .red) ||
1637  (c0.green != c1.green) ||
1638  (c0.blue != c1 .blue) ;
1639 }

1641 inline std::size_t hamming_distance(const rgb_t& c0, const rgb_t& c1)
1642 {
1643  std::size_t result = 0;
1644 
1645  if (c0.red != c1 .red) ++result;
1646  if (c0.green != c1.green) ++result;
1647  if (c0.blue != c1 .blue) ++result;
1648 
1649  return result;
1650 }

1652 inline rgb_t make_colour(const unsigned int& red, const unsigned int& green, const unsigned int& blue)
1653 {
1654  rgb_t result;
1655 
1656  result.red = static_cast<unsigned char>(red );
1657  result.green = static_cast<unsigned char>(green);
1658  result.blue = static_cast<unsigned char>(blue );
1659

1661 }

1663 template <typename OutputIterator>
1664 inline void generate_colours(const std::size_t& steps, const rgb_t c0, const rgb_t& c1, OutputIterator out)
1665 {
1666  double dr = ((double)c1.red - (double)c0.red ) / steps;
1667  double dg = ((double)c1.green - (double)c0.green ) / steps;
1668  double db = ((double)c1.blue - (double)c0.blue ) / steps;
1669 
1670  for (std::size_t i = 0; i < steps; ++i)
1671  {
1672  rgb_t c;
1673 
1674  c.red = static_cast<unsigned char>(c0.red + (i * dr));
1675  c.green = static_cast<unsigned char>(c0.green + (i * dg));
1676  c.blue = static_cast<unsigned char>(c0.blue + (i * db));
1677 
1678  *(out++) = c;
1679  }
1680 }

1682 template <typename ResponseImage, typename Palette>
1683 inline std::size_t convert_rsp_to_image(const ResponseImage& resp_image, const Palette& palette, bitmap_image& image)
1684 {
1685  if (
1686  (resp_image.width () > image.width ()) ||
1687  (resp_image.height() > image.height())
1688  )
1689  return 0;
1690 
1691  for (std::size_t y = 0; y < resp_image.height(); ++y)
1692  {
1693  for (std::size_t x = 0; x < resp_image.width(); ++x)
1694  {
1695  const double v = resp_image(x,y);
1696 
1697  unsigned int index = static_cast<unsigned int>((v < 0) ? 0 : v > (palette.size()) ? (palette.size() - 1) : v);
1698 
1699  image.set_pixel(x,y,palette[index]);
1700  }
1701  }
1702 
1703  return (resp_image.width() * resp_image.height());
1704 }

1706 inline void rgb_to_ycbcr(const unsigned int& length, double* red, double* green, double* blue,
1707  double* y, double* cb, double* cr)
1708 {
1709  unsigned int i = 0;
1710 
1711  while (i < length)
1712  {
1713  ( *y) = 16.0 + ( 65.481 * (*red) + 128.553 * (*green) + 24.966 * (*blue));
1714  (*cb) = 128.0 + ( -37.797 * (*red) + -74.203 * (*green) + 112.000 * (*blue));
1715  (*cr) = 128.0 + ( 112.000 * (*red) + -93.786 * (*green) - 18.214 * (*blue));
1716 
1717  ++i;
1718  ++red; ++green; ++blue;
1719  ++y; ++cb; ++cr;
1720  }
1721 }
1722 
1723 inline void ycbcr_to_rgb(const unsigned int& length, double* y, double* cb, double* cr,
1724  double* red, double* green, double* blue)
1725 {
1726  unsigned int i = 0;
1727 
1728  while (i < length)
1729  {
1730  double y_ = (*y) - 16.0;
1731  double cb_ = (*cb) - 128.0;
1732  double cr_ = (*cr) - 128.0;
1733 
1734  (*red) = 0.000456621 * y_ + 0.00625893 * cr_;
1735  (*green) = 0.000456621 * y_ - 0.00153632 * cb_ - 0.00318811 * cr_;
1736  (*blue) = 0.000456621 * y_ + 0.00791071 * cb_;
1737 
1738  ++i;
1739  ++red; ++green; ++blue;
1740  ++y; ++cb; ++cr;
1741  }
1742 }
1743 
1744 inline void subsample(const unsigned int& width,
1745  const unsigned int& height,
1746  const double* source,
1747  unsigned int& w,
1748  unsigned int& h,
1749  double*& dest)
1750 {
1751  /* Single channel. */
1752 
1753  w = 0;
1754  h = 0;
1755 
1756  bool odd_width = false;
1757  bool odd_height = false;
1758 
1759  if (0 == (width % 2))
1760  w = width / 2;
1761  else
1762  {
1763  w = 1 + (width / 2);
1764  odd_width = true;
1765  }
1766 
1767  if (0 == (height % 2))
1768  h = height / 2;
1769  else
1770  {
1771  h = 1 + (height / 2);
1772  odd_height = true;
1773  }
1774 
1775  unsigned int horizontal_upper = (odd_width) ? w - 1 : w;
1776  unsigned int vertical_upper = (odd_height) ? h - 1 : h;
1777 
1778  dest = new double[w * h];
1779 
1780  double* s_itr = dest;
1781  const double* itr1 = source;
1782  const double* itr2 = source + width;
1783 
1784  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < vertical_upper; ++j)
1785  {
1786  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i, ++s_itr)
1787  {
1788  (*s_itr) = *(itr1++);
1789  (*s_itr) += *(itr1++);
1790  (*s_itr) += *(itr2++);
1791  (*s_itr) += *(itr2++);
1792  (*s_itr) /= 4.0;
1793  }
1794 
1795  if (odd_width)
1796  {
1797  (*(s_itr++)) = ((*itr1++) + (*itr2++)) / 2.0;
1798  }
1799 
1800  itr1 += width;
1801 
1802  if (j != (vertical_upper -1))
1803  {
1804  itr2 += width;
1805  }
1806  }
1807 
1808  if (odd_height)
1809  {
1810  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < horizontal_upper; ++i, ++s_itr)
1811  {
1812  (*s_itr) += (*(itr1++));
1813  (*s_itr) += (*(itr1++));
1814  (*s_itr) /= 2.0;
1815  }
1816 
1817  if (odd_width)
1818  {
1819  (*(s_itr++)) = (*itr1);
1820  }
1821  }
1822 }
1823 
1824 inline void upsample(const unsigned int& width,
1825  const unsigned int& height,
1826  const double* source,
1827  unsigned int& w,
1828  unsigned int& h,
1829  double*& dest)
1830 {
1831  /* Single channel. */
1832 
1833  w = 2 * width;
1834  h = 2 * height;
1835 
1836  dest = new double[w * h];
1837 
1838  const double* s_itr = source;
1839  double* itr1 = dest;
1840  double* itr2 = dest + w;
1841 
1842  for (unsigned int j = 0; j < height; ++j)
1843  {
1844  for (unsigned int i = 0; i < width; ++i, ++s_itr)
1845  {
1846  *(itr1++) = (*s_itr);
1847  *(itr1++) = (*s_itr);
1848  *(itr2++) = (*s_itr);
1849  *(itr2++) = (*s_itr);
1850  }
1851 
1852  itr1 += w;
1853  itr2 += w;
1854  }
1855 }

1857 inline void checkered_pattern(const unsigned int x_width,
1858  const unsigned int y_width,
1859  const unsigned char value,
1860  const bitmap_image::color_plane color,
1861  bitmap_image& image)
1862 {
1863  if (
1864  (x_width >= image.width ()) ||
1865  (y_width >= image.height())
1866  )
1867  {
1868  return;
1869  }
1870 
1871  bool setter_x = false;
1872  bool setter_y = true;
1873 
1874  const unsigned int color_plane_offset = image.offset(color);
1875  const unsigned int height = image.height();
1876  const unsigned int width = image.width();
1877 
1878  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < height; ++y)
1879  {
1880  if (0 == (y % y_width))
1881  {
1882  setter_y = !setter_y;
1883  }
1884 
1885  unsigned char* row = image.row(y) + color_plane_offset;
1886 
1887  for (unsigned int x = 0; x < width; ++x, row += image.bytes_per_pixel())
1888  {
1889  if (0 == (x % x_width))
1890  {
1891  setter_x = !setter_x;
1892  }
1893 
1894  if (setter_x ^ setter_y)
1895  {
1896  *row = value;
1897  }
1898  }
1899  }
1900 }

1902 inline void checkered_pattern(const unsigned int x_width,
1903  const unsigned int y_width,
1904  const unsigned char red,
1905  const unsigned char green,
1906  const unsigned char blue,
1907  bitmap_image& image)
1908 {
1909  if (
1910  (x_width >= image.width ()) ||
1911  (y_width >= image.height())
1912  )
1913  {
1914  return;
1915  }
1916 
1917  bool setter_x = false;
1918  bool setter_y = true;
1919 
1920  const unsigned int height = image.height();
1921  const unsigned int width = image.width();
1922 
1923  for (unsigned int y = 0; y < height; ++y)
1924  {
1925  if (0 == (y % y_width))
1926  {
1927  setter_y = !setter_y;
1928  }
1929 
1930  unsigned char* row = image.row(y);
1931 
1932  for (unsigned int x = 0; x < width; ++x, row += image.bytes_per_pixel())
1933  {

1935  {
1936  setter_x = !setter_x;
1937  }
1938

1940  {
1941  *(row + 0) = blue;
1942  *(row + 1) = green;
1943  *(row + 2) = red;
1944  }
1945  }

1948 
1949 inline void plasma(bitmap_image& image,
1950  const double& x, const double& y,
1951  const double& width, const double& height,
1952  const double& c1, const double& c2,
1953  const double& c3, const double& c4,
1954  const double& roughness = 3.0,
1955  const rgb_t colormap[] = 0)
1956 {
1957  // Note: c1,c2,c3,c4 -> [0.0,1.0]
1958 
1959  const double half_width = ( width / 2.0);
1960  const double half_height = (height / 2.0);
1961 
1962  if ((width >= 1.0) || (height >= 1.0))
1963  {
1964  const double corner1 = (c1 + c2) / 2.0;
1965  const double corner2 = (c2 + c3) / 2.0;
1966  const double corner3 = (c3 + c4) / 2.0;
1967  const double corner4 = (c4 + c1) / 2.0;
1968  double center = (c1 + c2 + c3 + c4) / 4.0 +
1969  ((1.0 * ::rand() /(1.0 * RAND_MAX)) - 0.5) * // should use a better rng
1970  ((1.0 * half_width + half_height) / (image.width() + image.height()) * roughness);
1971 
1972  center = std::min<double>(std::max<double>(0.0,center),1.0);
1973 
1974  plasma(image, x, y, half_width, half_height, c1, corner1, center, corner4,roughness,colormap);
1975  plasma(image, x + half_width, y, half_width, half_height, corner1, c2, corner2, center,roughness,colormap);
1976  plasma(image, x + half_width, y + half_height, half_width, half_height, center, corner2, c3, corner3,roughness,colormap);
1977  plasma(image, x, y + half_height, half_width, half_height, corner4, center, corner3, c4,roughness,colormap);
1978  }
1979  else
1980  {
1981  rgb_t color = colormap[static_cast<unsigned int>(1000.0 * ((c1 + c2 + c3 + c4) / 4.0)) % 1000];
1982 
1983  image.set_pixel(static_cast<unsigned int>(x),static_cast<unsigned int>(y),color);
1984  }
1985 }
1986 
1987 inline void plasma(bitmap_image& image,
1988  const double& c1, const double& c2,
1989  const double& c3, const double& c4,
1990  const double& roughness = 3.0,
1991  const rgb_t colormap[] = 0)
1992 {
1993  plasma
1994  (
1995  image, 0, 0, image.width(), image.height(),
1996  c1, c2, c3, c4,
1997  roughness, colormap
1998  );
1999 }
2000 
2001 inline double psnr_region(const unsigned int& x, const unsigned int& y,
2002  const unsigned int& width, const unsigned int& height,
2003  const bitmap_image& image1, const bitmap_image& image2)
2004 {
2005  if (
2006  (image1.width() != image2.width ()) ||
2007  (image1.height() != image2.height())
2008  )
2009  {
2010  return 0.0;
2011  }
2012 
2013  if ((x + width ) > image1.width() ) { return 0.0; }
2014  if ((y + height) > image1.height()) { return 0.0; }
2015 
2016  double mse = 0.0;
2017 
2018  for (unsigned int r = 0; r < height; ++r)
2019  {
2020  const unsigned char* itr1 = image1.row(r + y) + x * image1.bytes_per_pixel();
2021  const unsigned char* itr1_end = itr1 + (width * image1.bytes_per_pixel());
2022  const unsigned char* itr2 = image2.row(r + y) + x * image2.bytes_per_pixel();
2023 
2024  while (itr1 != itr1_end)
2025  {
2026  double v = (static_cast<double>(*itr1) - static_cast<double>(*itr2));
2027  mse += v * v;
2028  ++itr1;
2029  ++itr2;
2030  }
2031  }
2032 
2033  if (mse <= 0.0000001)
2034  {
2035  return 1000000.0;
2036  }
2037  else
2038  {
2039  mse /= (3.0 * width * height);
2040  return 20.0 * std::log10(255.0 / std::sqrt(mse));
2041  }
2042 }
2043 
2044 inline void hierarchical_psnr_r(const double& x, const double& y,
2045  const double& width, const double& height,
2046  const bitmap_image& image1,
2047  bitmap_image& image2,
2048  const double& threshold,
2049  const rgb_t colormap[])
2050 {
2051  if ((width <= 4.0) || (height <= 4.0))
2052  {
2053  const double psnr = psnr_region
2054  (
2055  static_cast<unsigned int>(x),
2056  static_cast<unsigned int>(y),
2057  static_cast<unsigned int>(width),
2058  static_cast<unsigned int>(height),
2059  image1, image2
2060  );
2061 
2062  if (psnr < threshold)
2063  {
2064  rgb_t c = colormap[static_cast<unsigned int>(1000.0 * (1.0 - (psnr / threshold)))];
2065 
2066  image2.set_region
2067  (
2068  static_cast<unsigned int>(x),
2069  static_cast<unsigned int>(y),
2070  static_cast<unsigned int>(width + 1),
2071  static_cast<unsigned int>(height + 1),
2072  c.red, c.green, c.blue
2073  );
2074  }
2075  }
2076  else
2077  {
2078  const double half_width = ( width / 2.0);
2079  const double half_height = (height / 2.0);
2080 
2081  hierarchical_psnr_r(x , y , half_width, half_height, image1, image2, threshold, colormap);
2082  hierarchical_psnr_r(x + half_width, y , half_width, half_height, image1, image2, threshold, colormap);
2083  hierarchical_psnr_r(x + half_width, y + half_height, half_width, half_height, image1, image2, threshold, colormap);
2084  hierarchical_psnr_r(x , y + half_height, half_width, half_height, image1, image2, threshold, colormap);
2085  }
2086 }
2087 
2088 inline void hierarchical_psnr(bitmap_image& image1, bitmap_image& image2, const double threshold, const rgb_t colormap[])
2089 {
2090  if (
2091  (image1.width() != image2.width ()) ||
2092  (image1.height() != image2.height())
2093  )
2094  {
2095  return;
2096  }
2097 
2098  const double psnr = psnr_region
2099  (
2100  0, 0, image1.width(), image1.height(),
2101  image1, image2
2102  );
2103 
2104  if (psnr < threshold)
2105  {
2106  hierarchical_psnr_r
2107  (
2108  0, 0, image1.width(), image1.height(),
2109  image1, image2,
2110  threshold,
2111  colormap
2112  );
2113  }
2114 }

2116 class image_drawer
2117 {

2119

2121  : image_(image),
2122  pen_width_(1),
2123  pen_color_red_ (0),
2124  pen_color_green_(0),
2125  pen_color_blue_ (0)
2126  {}
2127 
2128  void rectangle(int x1, int y1, int x2, int y2)

2131  line_segment(x2, y1, x2, y2);
2132  line_segment(x2, y2, x1, y2);

2143  void quadix(int x1, int y1, int x2, int y2,int x3, int y3, int x4, int y4)
2144  {
2145  line_segment(x1, y1, x2, y2);
2146  line_segment(x2, y2, x3, y3);
2147  line_segment(x3, y3, x4, y4);
2148  line_segment(x4, y4, x1, y1);
2149  }
2150 
2151  void line_segment(int x1, int y1, int x2, int y2)
2152  {
2153  int steep = 0;
2154  int sx = ((x2 - x1) > 0) ? 1 : -1;
2155  int sy = ((y2 - y1) > 0) ? 1 : -1;
2156  int dx = abs(x2 - x1);
2157  int dy = abs(y2 - y1);
2158 
2159  if (dy > dx)
2160  {
2161  std::swap(x1,y1);
2162  std::swap(dx,dy);
2163  std::swap(sx,sy);
2164 
2165  steep = 1;
2166  }
2167 
2168  int e = 2 * dy - dx;
2169 
2170  for (int i = 0; i < dx; ++i)
2171  {
2172  if (steep)
2173  plot_pen_pixel(y1,x1);
2174  else
2175  plot_pen_pixel(x1,y1);
2176 
2177  while (e >= 0)
2178  {
2179  y1 += sy;
2180  e -= (dx << 1);
2181  }
2182 
2183  x1 += sx;
2184  e += (dy << 1);
2185  }
2186 
2187  plot_pen_pixel(x2,y2);
2188  }
2189 
2190  void horiztonal_line_segment(int x1, int x2, int y)
2191  {
2192  if (x1 > x2)
2193  {
2194  std::swap(x1,x2);
2195  }
2196 
2197  for (int i = 0; i < (x2 - x1); ++i)
2198  {
2199  plot_pen_pixel(x1 + i,y);
2200  }
2201  }
2202 
2203  void vertical_line_segment(int y1, int y2, int x)
2204  {
2205  if (y1 > y2)
2206  {
2207  std::swap(y1,y2);
2208  }
2209 
2210  for (int i = 0; i < (y2 - y1); ++i)
2211  {
2212  plot_pen_pixel(x, y1 + i);
2213  }
2214  }
2215 
2216  void ellipse(int centerx, int centery, int a, int b)
2217  {
2218  int t1 = a * a;
2219  int t2 = t1 << 1;
2220  int t3 = t2 << 1;
2221  int t4 = b * b;
2222  int t5 = t4 << 1;
2223  int t6 = t5 << 1;
2224  int t7 = a * t5;
2225  int t8 = t7 << 1;
2226  int t9 = 0;
2227 
2228  int d1 = t2 - t7 + (t4 >> 1);
2229  int d2 = (t1 >> 1) - t8 + t5;
2230  int x = a;
2231  int y = 0;
2232 
2233  int negative_tx = centerx - x;
2234  int positive_tx = centerx + x;
2235  int negative_ty = centery - y;
2236  int positive_ty = centery + y;
2237 
2238  while (d2 < 0)
2239  {
2240  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx, positive_ty);
2241  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx, negative_ty);
2242  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx, positive_ty);
2243  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx, negative_ty);
2244 
2245  ++y;
2246 
2247  t9 = t9 + t3;
2248 
2249  if (d1 < 0)
2250  {
2251  d1 = d1 + t9 + t2;
2252  d2 = d2 + t9;
2253  }
2254  else
2255  {
2256  x--;
2257  t8 = t8 - t6;
2258  d1 = d1 + (t9 + t2 - t8);
2259  d2 = d2 + (t9 + t5 - t8);
2260  negative_tx = centerx - x;
2261  positive_tx = centerx + x;
2262  }
2263 
2264  negative_ty = centery - y;
2265  positive_ty = centery + y;
2266  }
2267 
2268  do
2269  {
2270  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx, positive_ty);
2271  plot_pen_pixel(positive_tx, negative_ty);
2272  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx, positive_ty);
2273  plot_pen_pixel(negative_tx, negative_ty);
2274 
2275  x--;
2276  t8 = t8 - t6;
2277 
2278  if (d2 < 0)
2279  {
2280  ++y;
2281  t9 = t9 + t3;
2282  d2 = d2 + (t9 + t5 - t8);
2283  negative_ty = centery - y;
2284  positive_ty = centery + y;
2285  }
2286  else
2287  d2 = d2 + (t5 - t8);
2288 
2289  negative_tx = centerx - x;
2290  positive_tx = centerx + x;
2291  }
2292  while (x >= 0);
2293  }
2294 
2295  void circle(int centerx, int centery, int radius)
2296  {
2297  int x = 0;
2298  int d = (1 - radius) << 1;
2299 
2300  while (radius >= 0)
2301  {
2302  plot_pen_pixel(centerx + x, centery + radius);
2303  plot_pen_pixel(centerx + x, centery - radius);
2304  plot_pen_pixel(centerx - x, centery + radius);
2305  plot_pen_pixel(centerx - x, centery - radius);
2306 
2307  if ((d + radius) > 0)
2308  d -= ((--radius) << 1) - 1;
2309  if (x > d)
2310  d += ((++x) << 1) + 1;
2311  }
2312  }
2313 
2314  void plot_pen_pixel(int x, int y)
2315  {
2316  switch (pen_width_)
2317  {
2318  case 1 : plot_pixel(x,y);
2319  break;
2320 
2321  case 2 : {
2322  plot_pixel(x , y );
2323  plot_pixel(x + 1, y );
2324  plot_pixel(x + 1, y + 1);
2325  plot_pixel(x , y + 1);
2326  }
2327  break;
2328 
2329  case 3 : {
2330  plot_pixel(x , y - 1);
2331  plot_pixel(x - 1, y - 1);
2332  plot_pixel(x + 1, y - 1);
2333 
2334  plot_pixel(x , y );
2335  plot_pixel(x - 1, y );
2336  plot_pixel(x + 1, y );
2337 
2338  plot_pixel(x , y + 1);
2339  plot_pixel(x - 1, y + 1);
2340  plot_pixel(x + 1, y + 1);
2341  }
2342  break;
2343 
2344  default : plot_pixel(x,y);
2345  break;
2346  }
2347  }
2348 
2349  void plot_pixel(int x, int y)
2350  {
2351  if (
2352  (x < 0) ||
2353  (y < 0) ||
2354  (x >= static_cast<int>(image_.width ())) ||
2355  (y >= static_cast<int>(image_.height()))
2356  )
2357  return;
2358 
2359  image_.set_pixel(x,y,pen_color_red_,pen_color_green_,pen_color_blue_);
2360  }
2361 
2362  void pen_width(const unsigned int& width)
2363  {
2364  if ((width > 0) && (width < 4))
2365  {
2366  pen_width_ = width;
2367  }
2368  }
2369 
2370  void pen_color(const unsigned char& red,
2371  const unsigned char& green,
2372  const unsigned char& blue)
2373  {
2374  pen_color_red_ = red;
2375  pen_color_green_ = green;
2376  pen_color_blue_ = blue;
2377  }
2378 
2379  template <typename RGB>
2380  void pen_color(const RGB colour)
2381  {
2382  pen_color_red_ = colour.red;
2383  pen_color_green_ = colour.green;
2384  pen_color_blue_ = colour.blue;
2385  }
2386 
2387 private:
2388

2390  image_drawer& operator =(const image_drawer& id);
2391 
2392  bitmap_image& image_;
2393  unsigned int pen_width_;

2395  unsigned char pen_color_green_;
2396  unsigned char pen_color_blue_;
2397 };

2499  void fill_rectangle(double x1, double y1, double x2, double y2)
2500  {
2501  if (y1 > y2)
2502  std::swap(y1, y2);
2503 
2504  for (double y = y1; y <= y2; y += 0.5)
2505  {
2506  line_segment(x1, y, x2, y);
2507  }
2508  }
2509 
2510  void fill_triangle(double x1, double y1, double x2, double y2, double x3, double y3)
2511  {
2512  typedef std::pair<double,double> point_t;
2513 
2514  std::vector<point_t> p;
2515 
2516  p.push_back(std::make_pair(x1,y1));
2517  p.push_back(std::make_pair(x2,y2));
2518  p.push_back(std::make_pair(x3,y3));
2519 
2520  if (p[0].second > p[1].second)
2521  std::swap(p[0],p[1]);
2522  if (p[0].second > p[2].second)
2523  std::swap(p[0],p[2]);
2524  if (p[1].second > p[2].second)
2525  std::swap(p[1],p[2]);
2526 
2527  class draw_modes
2528  {
2529  private:
2530 
2531  cartesian_canvas& canvas;
2532 
2533  // Needed for incompetent and broken msvc compiler versions
2534  #ifdef _MSC_VER
2535  #pragma warning(push)
2536  #pragma warning(disable: 4822)
2537  #endif
2538  draw_modes& operator=(const draw_modes&);
2539  #ifdef _MSC_VER
2540  #pragma warning(pop)
2541  #endif
2542 
2543  public:
2544 
2545  draw_modes(cartesian_canvas& c)
2546  : canvas(c)
2547  {}
2548 
2549  void bottom(const point_t& p0, const point_t& p1, const point_t& p2)
2550  {
2551  const double m0 = (p1.first - p0.first) / (2.0 * (p1.second - p0.second));
2552  const double m1 = (p2.first - p0.first) / (2.0 * (p2.second - p0.second));
2553 
2554  double x0 = p0.first;
2555  double x1 = p0.first;
2556 
2557  for (double y = p0.second; y <= p1.second; y += 0.5)
2558  {
2559  canvas.horiztonal_line_segment(x0, x1, y);
2560 
2561  x0 += m0;
2562  x1 += m1;
2563  }
2564  }
2565 
2566  void top(const point_t& p0, const point_t& p1, const point_t& p2)
2567  {
2568  const double m0 = (p2.first - p0.first) / (2.0 * (p2.second - p0.second));
2569  const double m1 = (p2.first - p1.first) / (2.0 * (p2.second - p1.second));
2570 
2571  double x0 = p2.first;
2572  double x1 = p2.first;
2573 
2574  for (double y = p2.second; y >= p0.second; y -= 0.5)
2575  {
2576  canvas.horiztonal_line_segment(x0, x1, y);
2577 
2578  x0 -= m0;
2579  x1 -= m1;
2580  }
2581  }
2582  };
2583 
2584  draw_modes dm(*this);
2585 
2586  const double eps = 0.00001;
2587 
2588  if (std::abs(p[1].second - p[2].second) < eps)
2589  dm.bottom(p[0], p[1], p[2]);
2590  else if (std::abs(p[0].second - p[1].second) < eps)
2591  dm.top(p[0], p[1], p[2]);
2592  else
2593  {
2594  point_t p3;
2595 
2596  p3.first = (p[0].first + ((p[1].second - p[0].second) / (p[2].second - p[0].second)) * (p[2].first - p[0].first));
2597  p3.second = p[1].second;
2598 
2599  dm.bottom(p[0], p[1], p3 );
2600  dm.top (p[1], p3 , p[2]);
2601  }
2602  }
2603 
2604  void fill_quadix(double x1, double y1, double x2, double y2, double x3, double y3, double x4, double y4)
2605  {
2606  fill_triangle(x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3);
2607  fill_triangle(x1, y1, x3, y3, x4, y4);
2608  }

2610  void fill_circle(double cx, double cy, double radius)
2611  {
2612  const double delta = 1.0;
2613  double x = radius;
2614  double y = 0.0;
2615  double dx = delta - (2.0 * delta * radius);
2616  double dy = 0.0;
2617  double dr = 0.0;
2618 
2619  while (x >= y)
2620  {
2621  for (double i = cx - x; i <= cx + x; i += delta)
2622  {
2623  horiztonal_line_segment(cx - x, cx + x, cy + y);
2624  horiztonal_line_segment(cx - x, cx + x, cy - y);
2625  }
2626 
2627  for (double i = cx - y; i <= cx + y; i += delta)
2628  {
2629  horiztonal_line_segment(cx - y, cx + y, cy + x);
2630  horiztonal_line_segment(cx - y, cx + y, cy - x);
2631  }
2632 
2633  y += delta;
2634 
2635  dr += dy;
2636  dy += 2.0 * delta;
2637 
2638  if ((2.0 * delta * dr + dx) > 0)
2639  {
2640  x -= delta;
2641  dr += dx;
2642  dx += 2.0 * delta;
2643  }
2644  }
2645  }

2650  if ((y < min_y_) || (y > max_y_)) return;
2651 
2652  const int sc_x = static_cast<int>(cart_to_screen_x(x));
2653  const int sc_y = static_cast<int>(cart_to_screen_y(y));
2654 
2655  draw_.plot_pen_pixel(sc_x, sc_y);
2656  }

2709  void setup_canvas(const double x_length, const double y_length)
2710  {
2711  if ((x_length < 2.0) || (y_length < 2.0))
2712  return;
2713 
2714  width_div2_ = x_length / 2.0;
2715  height_div2_ = y_length / 2.0;
2716 
2717  min_x_ = -width_div2_ ;
2718  min_y_ = -height_div2_;
2719  max_x_ = width_div2_ ;
2720  max_y_ = height_div2_;
2721 
2722  image_.setwidth_height(static_cast<unsigned int>(x_length) + 1, static_cast<unsigned int>(y_length) + 1);
2723 
2724  image_.clear(0xFF);
2725  }

2727  double clamp_x(const double& x)
2728  {

2730  else if (x > max_x_) return max_x_;
2731  else return x;
2732  }
2733 
2734  double clamp_y(const double& y)
2735  {
2736  if (y < min_y_) return min_y_;
2737  else if (y > max_y_) return max_y_;
2738  else return y;
2739  }
2740 
2741  double cart_to_screen_x(const double& x)
2742  {
2743  return x + width_div2_;
2744  }
2745 
2746  double cart_to_screen_y(const double& y)
2747  {
2748  return height_div2_ - y;
2749  }
2750 
2751  enum clip_code
2752  {
2753  e_clip_bottom = 1,
2754  e_clip_top = 2,
2755  e_clip_left = 4,
2756  e_clip_right = 8
2757  };
2758 
2759  int out_code(
2760  const double& x, const double& y,
2761  const double& x1, const double& y1,
2762  const double& x2, const double& y2
2763  )
2764  {
2765  int result = 0;
2766  if (y < y1) result |= e_clip_bottom;
2767  else if (y > y2) result |= e_clip_top;
2768 
2769  if (x < x1) result |= e_clip_left;
2770  else if (x > x2) result |= e_clip_right;
2771 
2772  return result;
2773  }
2774 
2775  bool clip(double& x1, double& y1, double& x2, double& y2)
2776  {
2777  bool result = false;
2778  double x = 0.0;
2779  double y = 0.0;
2780 
2781  int outcode0 = out_code(x1, y1, min_x_, min_y_, max_x_, max_y_);
2782  int outcode1 = out_code(x2, y2, min_x_, min_y_, max_x_, max_y_);
2783  int outcodeout = 0;
2784 
2785  while ((outcode0 != 0) || (outcode1 != 0))
2786  {
2787  if ((outcode0 & outcode1) != 0)
2788  return result;
2789  else
2790  {
2791  if (outcode0 != 0)
2792  outcodeout = outcode0;
2793  else
2794  outcodeout = outcode1;
2795 
2796  double dx = (x2 - x1);
2797  double dy = (y2 - y1);
2798 
2799  if ((outcodeout & e_clip_bottom) == e_clip_bottom)
2800  {
2801  x = x1 + dx * (min_y_ - y1) / dy;
2802  y = min_y_;
2803  }
2804  else if ((outcodeout & e_clip_top) == e_clip_top)
2805  {
2806  x = x1 + dx * (max_y_ - y1) / dy;
2807  y = max_y_;
2808  }
2809  else if ((outcodeout & e_clip_right) == e_clip_right)
2810  {
2811  y = y1 + dy * (max_x_ - x1) / dx;
2812  x = max_x_;
2813  }
2814  else if ((outcodeout & e_clip_left) == e_clip_left)
2815  {
2816  y = y1 + dy * (min_x_ - x1) / dx;
2817  x = min_x_;
2818  }
2819 
2820  if (outcodeout == outcode0)
2821  {
2822  x1 = x;
2823  y1 = y;
2824  outcode0 = out_code(x1, y1, min_x_, min_y_, max_x_, max_y_);
2825  }
2826  else
2827  {
2828  x2 = x;
2829  y2 = y;
2830  outcode1 = out_code(x2, y2, min_x_, min_y_, max_x_, max_y_);
2831  }
2832  }
2833  }
2834 
2835  return true;
2836  }
2837 
2838  cartesian_canvas(const cartesian_canvas&);
2839  cartesian_canvas operator=(const cartesian_canvas&);
2840 
2841  double width_div2_;
2842  double height_div2_;
2843  double min_x_;
2844  double min_y_;
2845  double max_x_;
2846  double max_y_;
2847  bitmap_image image_;
2848  image_drawer draw_;
2849 };
2850 
2851 inline rgb_t convert_wave_length_nm_to_rgb(const double wave_length_nm)
2852 {
2853  // Credits: Dan Bruton http://www.physics.sfasu.edu/astro/color.html
2854  double red = 0.0;
2855  double green = 0.0;
2856  double blue = 0.0;
2857 
2858  if ((380.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 439.0))
2859  {
2860  red = -(wave_length_nm - 440.0) / (440.0 - 380.0);
2861  green = 0.0;
2862  blue = 1.0;
2863  }
2864  else if ((440.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 489.0))
2865  {
2866  red = 0.0;
2867  green = (wave_length_nm - 440.0) / (490.0 - 440.0);
2868  blue = 1.0;
2869  }
2870  else if ((490.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 509.0))
2871  {
2872  red = 0.0;
2873  green = 1.0;
2874  blue = -(wave_length_nm - 510.0) / (510.0 - 490.0);
2875  }
2876  else if ((510.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 579.0))
2877  {
2878  red = (wave_length_nm - 510.0) / (580.0 - 510.0);
2879  green = 1.0;
2880  blue = 0.0;
2881  }
2882  else if ((580.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 644.0))
2883  {
2884  red = 1.0;
2885  green = -(wave_length_nm - 645.0) / (645.0 - 580.0);
2886  blue = 0.0;
2887  }
2888  else if ((645.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 780.0))
2889  {
2890  red = 1.0;
2891  green = 0.0;
2892  blue = 0.0;
2893  }
2894 
2895  double factor = 0.0;
2896 
2897  if ((380.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 419.0))
2898  factor = 0.3 + 0.7 * (wave_length_nm - 380.0) / (420.0 - 380.0);
2899  else if ((420.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 700.0))
2900  factor = 1.0;
2901  else if ((701.0 <= wave_length_nm) && (wave_length_nm <= 780.0))
2902  factor = 0.3 + 0.7 * (780.0 - wave_length_nm) / (780.0 - 700.0);
2903  else
2904  factor = 0.0;
2905 
2906  rgb_t result;
2907 
2908  const double gamma = 0.8;
2909  const double intensity_max = 255.0;
2910 
2911  #define round(d) std::floor(d + 0.5)
2912 
2913  result.red = static_cast<unsigned char>((red == 0.0) ? red : round(intensity_max * std::pow(red * factor, gamma)));
2914  result.green = static_cast<unsigned char>((green == 0.0) ? green : round(intensity_max * std::pow(green * factor, gamma)));
2915  result.blue = static_cast<unsigned char>((blue == 0.0) ? blue : round(intensity_max * std::pow(blue * factor, gamma)));
2916 
2917  #undef round
2918 
2919  return result;
2920 }
2921 
2922 inline double weighted_distance(const unsigned char r0, const unsigned char g0, const unsigned char b0,
2923  const unsigned char r1, const unsigned char g1, const unsigned char b1)
2924 {
2925  const double diff_r = /*0.30 */ (r0 - r1);
2926  const double diff_g = /*0.59 */ (g0 - g1);
2927  const double diff_b = /*0.11 */ (b0 - b1);
2928 
2929  return std::sqrt((diff_r * diff_r) + (diff_g * diff_g) + (diff_b * diff_b));
2930 }
2931 
2932 inline double weighted_distance(const rgb_t c0, const rgb_t c1)
2933 {
2934  return weighted_distance(c0.red, c0.green, c0.blue,
2935  c1.red, c1.green, c1.blue);
2936 }
2937 
2938 template <typename Iterator>
2939 inline rgb_t find_nearest_color(const rgb_t& c, const Iterator begin, const Iterator end)
2940 {
2941  if (0 == std::distance(begin,end))
2942  return c;
2943 
2944  double min_d = std::numeric_limits<double>::max();
2945  rgb_t result = *begin;
2946 
2947  for (Iterator itr = begin; itr != end; ++itr)
2948  {
2949  if (c == (*itr))
2950  {
2951  return (*itr);
2952  }
2953 
2954  double curr_d = weighted_distance(c,*itr);
2955 
2956  if (curr_d < min_d)
2957  {
2958  min_d = curr_d;
2959  result = *itr;
2960  }
2961  }
2962 
2963  return result;
2964 }
2965 
2966 template <template <typename,typename> class Sequence,
2967  typename Allocator>
2968 inline rgb_t find_nearest_color(const rgb_t& c, const Sequence<rgb_t,Allocator>& seq)
2969 {
2970  return find_nearest_color(c, seq.begin(),seq.end());
2971 }
2972 
2973 template <std::size_t N>
2974 inline rgb_t find_nearest_color(const rgb_t& c, const rgb_t (&colors)[N])
2975 {
2976  return find_nearest_color(c, colors, colors + N);
2977 }

2979 inline double find_nearest_wave_length(const rgb_t& c, const double increment = 0.001)
2980 {
2981  const double max_wave_length = 800.0; //800nm
2982 
2983  double min_wave_length = 0.0;
2984  double min_d = std::numeric_limits<double>::max();
2985 
2986  for (double i = 0.0; i < max_wave_length; i += increment)
2987  {
2988  const rgb_t curr_rgb = convert_wave_length_nm_to_rgb(i);
2989 
2990  if (c == curr_rgb)
2991  {
2992  return i;
2993  }
2994 
2995  const double curr_d = weighted_distance(c, curr_rgb);
2996 
2997  if (curr_d <= min_d)
2998  {
2999  min_wave_length = i;
3000  min_d = curr_d;
3001  }
3002  }
3003 
3004  return min_wave_length;
3005 }

3007 template <typename T>
3008 class response_image
3009 {
3010 public:
3011 
3012  response_image(const std::size_t& width, const std::size_t& height, const T null = T(0))
3013  : width_ (width ),
3014  height_(height),
3015  null_ (null )
3016  {
3017  data_.resize(width_ * height_);
3018  }
3019 
3020  std::size_t width () const { return width_; }
3021  std::size_t height() const { return height_; }
3022 
3023  void set_all(const T& t)
3024  {
3025  std::fill_n(data_.begin(), data_.size(), t);
3026  }
3027 
3028  const T& operator()(const std::size_t& x, const std::size_t& y) const
3029  {
3030  if (y >= height_) return null_;
3031  if (x >= width_ ) return null_;
3032 
3033  return data_[width_ * y + x];
3034  }
3035 
3036  T& operator()(const std::size_t& x, const std::size_t& y)
3037  {
3038  if (y >= height_) return null_;
3039  if (x >= width_ ) return null_;
3040 
3041  return data_[width_ * y + x];
3042  }
3043 
3044  bool valid(const std::size_t& x, const std::size_t& y)
3045  {
3046  return ((x < width_ ) || (y < height_));
3047  }
3048 
3049  void inc_all(const T& v)
3050  {
3051  for (std::size_t i = 0; i < data_.size(); ++i)
3052  {
3053  data_[i] += v;
3054  }
3055  }
3056 
3057  void mul_all(const T& v)
3058  {
3059  for (std::size_t i = 0; i < data_.size(); ++i)
3060  {
3061  data_[i] *= v;
3062  }
3063  }
3064 
3065  T* row (const std::size_t& row_index)
3066  {
3067  if (row_index < height_)
3068  return &data_[width_ * row_index];
3069  else
3070  return reinterpret_cast<T*>(0);
3071  }
3072 
3073  const T* row (const std::size_t& row_index) const
3074  {
3075  if (row_index < height_)
3076  return data_[width_ * row_index];
3077  else
3078  return reinterpret_cast<T*>(0);
3079  }
3080 
3081 private:
3082 
3083  std::size_t width_;
3084  std::size_t height_;
3085  std::vector<T> data_;
3086  T null_;
3087 };

3089 inline void sobel_operator(const bitmap_image& src_image,
3090  bitmap_image& dst_image,
3091  const double threshold = 0.0)
3092 {
3093  typedef double T;
3094 
3095  response_image<T> im0(src_image.width(), src_image.height(), 0.0);
3096  response_image<T> im1(src_image.width(), src_image.height(), 0.0);
3097 
3098  src_image.export_gray_scale_response_image(&im0(0,0));
3099 
3100  for (std::size_t y = 1; y < im0.height() - 1; ++y)
3101  {
3102  const T* itr0 = im0.row(y - 1);
3103  const T* itr1 = im0.row(y );
3104  const T* itr2 = im0.row(y + 1);
3105  T* out = im1.row(y ) + 1;
3106 
3107  for (std::size_t x = 1; x < im0.width() - 1; ++x)
3108  {
3109  const T c0 = *(itr0 + x - 1); const T c1 = *(itr0 + x); const T c2 = *(itr0 + x + 1);
3110  const T c3 = *(itr1 + x - 1); /*const T c4 = *(itr1 + x);*/ const T c5 = *(itr1 + x + 1);
3111  const T c6 = *(itr2 + x - 1); const T c7 = *(itr2 + x); const T c8 = *(itr2 + x + 1);
3112 
3113  const T gx = (2.0 * (c5 - c3)) + (c2 - c0) + (c8 - c6);
3114  const T gy = (2.0 * (c1 - c7)) + (c0 - c6) + (c2 - c8);
3115 
3116  *(out++) = std::sqrt((gx * gx) + (gy * gy));
3117  }
3118  }
3119 
3120  if (threshold > 0.0)
3121  {
3122  const T* end = im1.row(0) + (im1.width() * im1.height());
3123 
3124  for (T* itr = im1.row(0); itr != end; ++itr)
3125  {
3126  T& v = *itr;
3127  if (v <= threshold) v = 0;
3128  }
3129  }
3130 
3131  dst_image.setwidth_height
3132  (
3133  static_cast<unsigned int>(im1.width()),
3134  static_cast<unsigned int>(im1.height())
3135  );
3136 
3137  dst_image.import_gray_scale_clamped(&im1(0,0));
3138 }
